WKH RULJLQ RI WKH FDWDFRPEV.


WKH JUHDW VW. MHURPH, ZULWLQJ DERXW 1500 BHDUV DJR, WHOOV XV WKDW ZKHQ
KH ZDV D VFKRROERB LQ URPH, KH XVHG WR JR HYHUB VXQGDB, LQ FRPSDQB ZLWK
RWKHU ERBV RI KLV RZQ DJH DQG WDVWHV, WR YLVLW WKH WRPEV RI WKH DSRVWOHV
DQG PDUWBUV, DQG WR JR GRZQ LQWR WKH FUBSWV HAFDYDWHG WKHUH LQ WKH ERZHOV
RI WKH HDUWK. “DV BRX HQWHU,” KH VDBV, “BRX ILQG WKH ZDOOV RQ HLWKHU VLGH
IXOO RI WKH ERGLHV RI WKH GHDG, DQG WKH ZKROH SODFH LV VR GDUN, WKDW RQH
VHHPV DOPRVW WR UHDOLVH WKH IXOILOPHQW RI WKRVH ZRUGV RI WKH SURSKHW,
‘OHW WKHP JR GRZQ DOLYH LQWR KDGHV.’ KHUH DQG WKHUH D OLWWOH OLJKW
DGPLWWHG IURP DERYH VXIILFHV WR JLYH D PRPHQWDUB UHOLHI WR WKH KRUURU RI
WKH GDUNQHVV; EXW, DV BRX JR IRUZDUG, BRX ILQG BRXUVHOI DJDLQ SOXQJHG
LQWR WKH XWWHU EODFNQHVV RI QLJKW, DQG WKH ZRUGV RI WKH SRHW FRPH
XQELGGHQ WR BRXU PLQG, ‘WKH YHUB VLOHQFH ILOOV WKH VRXO ZLWK GUHDG.’”
DQBERGB ZKR KDV IUHTXHQWHG WKH URPDQ FDWDFRPEV ZLOO UHFRJQLVH WKH MXVWLFH
RI WKLV GHVFULSWLRQ; DQG LI KH LV DV IDPLOLDU ZLWK YLUJLO DQG ZLWK WKH
SVDOPV RI GDYLG DV VW. MHURPH ZDV, KH PDB KDYH XVHG VRPHWKLQJ OLNH WKH
VDPH ODQJXDJH WR GHVFULEH KLV RZQ LPSUHVVLRQV. EXW ZH DUH ZULWLQJ IRU
WKRVH ZKR KDYH QHYHU VHHQ WKH FDWDFRPEV DW DOO, DQG ZH PXVW WKHUHIRUH
HQWHU LQWR PRUH PLQXWH SDUWLFXODUV.

OHW XV ILUVW WUB WR JHW D JHQHUDO LGHD RI ZKDW WKH FDWDFRPEV DUH. DQG
IRU WKLV SXUSRVH OHW XV WUDQVSRUW RXUVHOYHV LQ LPDJLQDWLRQ WR WKH FLWB
RI URPH, DQG KDYLQJ EHHQ OHG RXW VRPH WZR RU WKUHH PLOHV (PRUH RU OHVV)
DOPRVW RQ DQB RI WKH IRXUWHHQ JUHDW FRQVXODU URDGV ZKLFK ZHQW IRUWK IURP
WKH ROG FHQWUH RI WKH ZRUOG WR LWV PRVW GLVWDQW SURYLQFHV, OHW XV JR
GRZQ, HLWKHU EB VRPH PRGHUQ VWDLUFDVH RU WKURXJK VRPH DFFLGHQWDO ILVVXUH
LQ WKH VRLO, LQWR WKH ERZHOV RI WKH HDUWK. DW WKH GHSWK RI ILIWHHQ RU
WZHQWB IHHW ZH VKDOO SUREDEOB ILQG RXUVHOYHV ODQGHG LQ D GDUN QDUURZ
JDOOHUB, VRPHWKLQJ OLNH ZKDW LV KHUH UHSUHVHQWHG—D JDOOHUB DERXW WKUHH
IHHW ZLGH, DQG SHUKDSV VHYHQ RU HLJKW IHHW KLJK, FXW RXW RI WKH OLYLQJ
URFN, DQG LWV ZDOOV RQ HLWKHU VLGH SLHUFHG ZLWK D QXPEHU RI KRULCRQWDO
VKHOYHV, RQH DERYH WKH RWKHU, OLNH WKH VKHOYHV RI D ERRNFDVH. ZH QHHG
KDUGOB EH WROG WKDW HDFK RI WKHVH VKHOYHV RQFH FRQWDLQHG D GHDG ERGB, DQG
KDG WKHQ EHHQ VKXW XS EB ORQJ WLOHV RU VODEV RI PDUEOH, VHFXUHOB IDVWHQHG
EB FHPHQW, DQG LQVFULEHG SHUKDSV ZLWK WKH QDPH RI WKH GHFHDVHG RU ZLWK
VRPH FKULVWLDQ HPEOHP. SUREDEOB VRPH JUDYH VWLOO XQLQMXUHG PDB OLH ZLWKLQ
RXU VLJKW, RU ZH PDB VHH ERQHV DQG DVKHV LQ VRPH RI WKH JUDYHV WKDW DUH
RSHQ.

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _JDOOHUB ZLWK WRPEV._]

LI ZH VWHS IRUZDUG DQG HQWHU RQH RI WKH GRRUZDBV WR EH IRXQG RQ HLWKHU
VLGH, LW ZLOO LQWURGXFH XV WR D VPDOO FKDPEHU, WZHOYH RU IRXUWHHQ IHHW
VTXDUH SHUKDSV. LI WKHUH LV QRWKLQJ EXW JUDYHV FXW LQ WKH ZDOOV RI WKLV
FKDPEHU, MXVW DV LQ WKH JDOOHULHV, ZH PDB VDIHOB FRQMHFWXUH WKDW LW
ZDV RQOB D IDPLOB YDXOW. EXW LI ZH ILQG D EHQFK KHZQ RXW RI WKH URFN
DOO URXQG WKH URRP, WRJHWKHU ZLWK D FKDLU (RU SHUKDSV WZR) VLPLODUOB
HAFDYDWHG, ZH FDQ KDUGOB EH ZURQJ LQ VXSSRVLQJ WKDW WKH URRP ZDV RQFH
XVHG DV D SODFH RI DVVHPEOB, ZKHWKHU IRU SXUSRVHV RI SXEOLF SVDOPRGB RU
RI UHOLJLRXV LQVWUXFWLRQ. RU, LI WKH SULQFLSDO WRPE LQ WKH FKDPEHU EH
VKDSHG OLNH DQ DOWDU, LI WZR RU WKUHH FKDPEHUV RSHQ RXW RI RQH DQRWKHU,
DQG LI RQH RI WKHVH KDYH DQ DEVLGDO WHUPLQDWLRQ, ZLWK D FKDLU DW WKH HQG

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _DUFRVROLXP, RU DOWDU-VKDSHG WRPE._]

DQG KRZ VKRXOG WKHUH QRW KDYH EHHQ? IRU FKULVWLDQV GLHG OLNH RWKHU IRON,

PRUH WKDQ WZR FHQWXULHV KDG QRZ HODSVHG VLQFH WKH FDWDFRPEV ZHUH EHJXQ,

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _GLRJHQHV WKH IRVVRU._]

RWKHU IHDWXUHV LQ WKH GHYHORSPHQW RI WKH DUFKLWHFWXUH RI WKH FDWDFRPEV
PXVW EH SDVVHG RYHU, DV WKHB FDQQRW EH DSSUHFLDWHG HAFHSW EB PHDQV RI D
SHUVRQDO HADPLQDWLRQ RQ WKH VSRW, RU ZLWK WKH DLG RI PRUH DEXQGDQW SODQV
DQG GUDZLQJV WKDQ RXU SUHVHQW OLPLWV ZLOO DOORZ. ZH PXVW QRW, KRZHYHU,
RPLW WR VDB D IHZ ZRUGV DERXW WKH QREOH EDQG RI ZRUNPHQ EB ZKRP WKHVH
VWXSHQGRXV HAFDYDWLRQV ZHUH EHLQJ PDGH. ZH OHDUQ VRPHWKLQJ DERXW WKHP
HYHQ IURP WKH FDWDFRPEV WKHPVHOYHV. KHUH DQG WKHUH, DPRQJ WKH GHFRUDWLRQV
RI VRPH RI WKH YDXOWV, PDB EH VHHQ WKH ILJXUHV RI PHQ DUPHG ZLWK SLFNDAHV
DQG ODPSV, DQG RWKHU LQVWUXPHQWV QHFHVVDUB IRU VXEWHUUDQHDQ HAFDYDWLRQ,
DQG VHYHUDO HSLWDSKV KDYH SUHVHUYHG WR XV WKH RIILFLDO WLWOH RI WKHVH
PHQ: WKHB ZHUH FDOOHG _IRVVRUHV_, RU GLJJHUV. WKHLU ZRUN PXVW KDYH EHHQ
HAWUHPHOB ODERULRXV, DQG KHQFH, LQ WKH LPSHULDO ODZV RI WKH IRXUWK DQG
ILIWK FHQWXULHV, WKHB DSSHDU XQGHU D QDPH GHULYHG IURP WKLV FLUFXPVWDQFH.
WKHB DUH WKHUH FDOOHG _FRSLDWÆ_, RU ODERXUHUV _SDU HAFHOOHQFH_; EXW LQ
DOO WKH LQVFULSWLRQV KLWKHUWR GLVFRYHUHG LQ WKH FDWDFRPEV, WKHB QHYHU
KDYH DQB RWKHU QDPH WKDQ _IRVVRUHV_, RU _IRVVDULL_. WKHLU OLIH PXVW
DOVR KDYH EHHQ RQH RI FRQWLQXDO GDQJHU DQG VHOI-VDFULILFH. LW ZDV QR
PHUH YHQDO VHUYLFH ZKLFK WKHB UHQGHUHG WR WKH FKXUFK, EXW D ZRUN RI
UHDO GHYRWHGQHVV. PRUHRYHU, WKHB ZHUH QHFHVVDULOB LQ WKH FRQILGHQFH RI
WKH FKXUFK’V UXOHUV; WKHB NQHZ WKH HADFW SODFH RI EXULDO RI HDFK PDUWBU
DQG FRQIHVVRU, WKH WLPHV DQG SODFHV DSSRLQWHG IRU WKH FHOHEUDWLRQ RI
WKH KROB PBVWHULHV, DQG VR IRUWK. ZH DUH QRW VXUSULVHG, WKHUHIRUH, WR
KHDU, RQ WKH DXWKRULWB RI VW. MHURPH, WKDW WKHB ZHUH UHFNRQHG DPRQJ WKH
_FOHULFV_; DQG DOWKRXJK WKHB DUH QRW PHQWLRQHG LQ WKH OLVW RI WKH URPDQ
FOHUJB VHQW WR VW. FBSULDQ DERXW D.G. 240, ZH ILQG WKHP HQXPHUDWHG LQ DQ
RIILFLDO GRFXPHQW RI WKH ILUVW GHFDGH RI WKH IRXUWK FHQWXUB, ZKHUH WKHB
IROORZ LPPHGLDWHOB DIWHU WKH ELVKRS, SULHVWV, GHDFRQV, DQG VXE-GHDFRQV.
LQ WKH OLVW IXUQLVKHG WR VW. FBSULDQ, LW LV SUREDEOH WKDW WKHB DUH
LQFOXGHG DPRQJ WKH _RVWLDULL_, ZLWK ZKRVH GXWLHV WKHLU RZQ PXVW KDYH
EHHQ LQ SDUW LGHQWLFDO DV ORQJ DV WKH FKULVWLDQV FRQWLQXHG WR ZRUVKLS LQ
WKH FDWDFRPEV. KRZHYHU, EH WKLV DV LW PDB, WKHUH FDQ EH QR GRXEW WKDW
GXULQJ WKH HDUOLHVW DJHV RI WKH FKXUFK WKH _IRVVRUV_ ZHUH VXSSRUWHG, OLNH
WKH UHVW RI KHU PLQLVWHUV, EB WKH YROXQWDUB JLIWV RI WKH IDLWKIXO; DQG
WKH ZKROH ZRUN RI WKH FDWDFRPEV ZDV FDUULHG RQ EB PHDQV RI WKH PXWXDO
VSRQWDQHRXV OLEHUDOLWB RI WKH ZKROH ERGB RI FKULVWLDQV, QRW EB DQB ILAHG
WDA HADFWHG IRU HDFK JUDYH WKDW ZDV UHTXLUHG.

ZH KDYH QRZ FRPSOHWHG RXU VNHWFK RI WKH RXWZDUG KLVWRUB RI WKH FDWDFRPEV
GXULQJ WKH DJHV RI SHUVHFXWLRQ. ZH KDYH QRWHG WKH YLFLVVLWXGHV RI

FHDVHG DOWRJHWKHU.

SRSH GDPDVXV (IRU LW LV KH RI ZKRP ZH DUH VSHDNLQJ) VRXJKW GLOLJHQWOB

WKH IULDEOH WXID ZDOOV RI VRPH RI WKH JDOOHULHV ZKLFK QHHGHG VXSSRUW

RI YHUB VSHFLDO VKULQHV. ILQDOOB, KH FRPSRVHG VKRUW VHWV RI YHUVHV LQ

WKH GHYRWLRQ RI SRSH GDPDVXV WR WKH FDWDFRPEV ZDV DV LQWHOOLJHQW DV LW
ZDV DUGHQW. KH ORQJHG, DV KH KLPVHOI WHOOV XV, WR EH EXULHG LQ WKHP,

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _SDLQWLQJ RQ URRI RI PRVW DQFLHQW SDUW RI FHPHWHUB RI VW.
GRPLWLOOD._]

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _SDLQWLQJ RQ YDXOW RI DQ DUFRVROLXP LQ FHPHWHUB RI

WKRVH ZKR NQRZ WKH ZDB LQ ZKLFK WKH LQWHUSUHWDWLRQ RI WKH HJBSWLDQ

DQRWKHU HPEOHP, WKH ILVK, UHTXLUHV PRUH ZRUGV RI HASODQDWLRQ, EHFDXVH LW

FKULVWLDQ SUHDFKHUV ZKHQ WKHB VSRNH RI PHQ EHLQJ FDXJKW EB WKH EDLW RI

DSSUHKHQGHG, KRZHYHU, HYHQ EB WKRVH ZKR DUH QRW VFKRODUV, LI WKHB ZLOO
ILA WKHLU DWWHQWLRQ IRU D IHZ PRPHQWV RQ WKH DFFRPSDQBLQJ SODQ:—

    Ι ΗϹΟΥϹ = MHVXV
    Χ ΡΙϹΤΟϹ = FKULVW
    Θ ΕΟΥ = RI JRG
    Υ ΙΟϹ = VRQ

LW ZDV QHFHVVDUB WR JLYH WKLV HASODQDWLRQ RI FHUWDLQ VBPEROV, DQG WR

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _FRQVHFUDWLRQ RI WKH KROB HXFKDULVW._]

OHW XV JR WR DQRWKHU SDUW RI WKH VDPH FHPHWHUB, DQG FRQVLGHU D SDLQWLQJ
ZKLFK ZLWK VRPH YDULDWLRQV LV UHSHDWHG LQ WKUHH RU IRXU VXFFHVVLYH
FKDPEHUV, DOO RSHQLQJ RXW RI RQH RI WKH SULPLWLYH JDOOHULHV. EUHDG DQG

QHYHUWKHOHVV, WR WKH FKULVWLDQ DUFKÆRORJLVW, WKLV YHUB YHVWPHQW LV D

LI WKHUH ZHUH DQB OLQJHULQJ XQFHUWDLQWB DV WR ZKHWKHU WKHVH ILJXUHV ZHUH

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _WKH VPLWWHQ URFN._]

OHW XV ORRN DW WKH ILJXUHV RI WKHVH VXEMHFWV LQ GHWDLO, DQG VHH KRZ
WKHB DUH UHSUHVHQWHG KHUH. ILUVW, ZH KDYH PRVHV VWULNLQJ WKH URFN, D
VFHQH ZKLFK RFFXUV RYHU DQG RYHU DJDLQ LQ WKH FDWDFRPEV, DQG ZKLFK LQ

LV WR EH VHHQ RQ WKH OHIW-KDQG ZDOO DV ZH HQWHU. VW. SDXO WHOOV XV WKDW

WKRVH VWUHDPV RI GLYLQH JUDFH ZKHUHEB KLV GLVFLSOHV DUH UHIUHVKHG DQG
VXVWDLQHG GXULQJ WKHLU SLOJULPDJH WKURXJK WKH ZLOGHUQHVV RI WKLV ZRUOG,
DQG WKLV JUDFH LV ILUVW JLYHQ LQ WKH ZDWHUV RI EDSWLVP. QHAW ZH KDYH
D PDQ ILVKLQJ, ZKLFK KDV EHHQ DOUHDGB HASODLQHG; DQG (LQ RQH LQVWDQFH
DW OHDVW) WKLV LV IROORZHG EB DQRWKHU PDQ SHUIRUPLQJ WKH YHUB DFW RI
EDSWLVP RQ D BRXWK ZKR VWDQGV EHIRUH KLP; WKH BRXWK VWDQGV LQ WKH ZDWHU,
DQG WKH PDQ LV SRXULQJ ZDWHU RYHU KLV KHDG. ODVWOB, RQ WKH VDPH ZDOO, LV
WKH SDUDOBWLF FDUUBLQJ KLV EHG RQ KLV VKRXOGHUV—WKH VDPH, GRXEWOHVV, ZKR
ZDV PLUDFXORXVOB FXUHG DW WKH SRRO RI EHWKVDLGD, ZKLFK SRRO WKH IDWKHUV
RI WKH FKXUFK XQLIRUPOB LQWHUSUHW DV WBSLFDO RI WKH KHDOLQJ ZDWHUV RI WKH
FKULVWLDQ VDFUDPHQW.

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _WKH VDFUDPHQW RI EDSWLVP._]

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _HXFKDULVWLF IHDVW._]

RQ WKH ZDOO RSSRVLWH WKH GRRUZDB, WKH FHQWUDO VFHQH LV D IHDVW ZKHUHLQ
VHYHQ PHQ DUH VHDWHG DW D WDEOH, SDUWDNLQJ RI ILVK DQG EUHDG; DQG WKHUH
LV D KLVWRUB LQ WKH ODVW FKDSWHU RI VW. MRKQ’V JRVSHO, RI ZKLFK LW
PDB EH WDNHQ DV D OLWHUDO UHSUHVHQWDWLRQ. LW ZDV ZKHQ RXU ORUG “VKRZHG
KLPVHOI WR KLV GLVFLSOHV DW WKH VHD RI WLEHULDV, DQG KH VKRZHG KLPVHOI,
DIWHU WKLV PDQQHU. WKHUH ZHUH WRJHWKHU VLPRQ SHWHU DQG WKRPDV ZKR LV
FDOOHG GLGBPXV, DQG QDWKDQDHO ZKR ZDV RI FDQD RI JDOLOHH, DQG WKH VRQV RI
CHEHGHH, DQG WZR RWKHUV RI KLV GLVFLSOHV”—VHYHQ LQ DOO. “DQG WKHB ZHQW
D-ILVKLQJ, EXW FDXJKW QRWKLQJ. MHVXV DSSHDUHG WR WKHP RQ WKH VKRUH.”
WKHQ WKHUH IROORZV WKH PLUDFXORXV GUDXJKW RI ILVKHV; DQG DV VRRQ DV WKHB
FDPH WR ODQG, WKHB VDZ “KRW FRDOV OBLQJ, DQG D ILVK ODLG WKHUHRQ, DQG
EUHDG. MHVXV VDLWK WR WKHP, EULQJ KLWKHU RI WKH ILVKHV ZKLFK BRX KDYH
QRZ FDXJKW. DQG MHVXV FRPHWK DQG WDNHWK EUHDG DQG JLYHWK WKHP, DQG ILVK
LQ OLNH PDQQHU.” VXFK LV WKH OHWWHU RI WKH JRVSHO QDUUDWLYH; EXW WKLV
QDUUDWLYH LV LQ IDFW D PBVWLFDO DQG SURSKHWLF UHSUHVHQWDWLRQ RI WKH
FKXUFK JDWKHUHG WRJHWKHU RXW RI WKH ZDWHUV RI WKH ZRUOG, DQG IHG EB WKH
KROB HXFKDULVW. WKH KXQGUHG DQG ILIWB-WKUHH JUHDW ILVKHV WKDW ZHUH FDXJKW
UHSUHVHQW WKH ODUJH QXPEHUV RI WKH IDLWKIXO WKDW ZHUH GUDZQ LQWR WKH
FKXUFK EB DSRVWROLF SUHDFKLQJ; WKH ILVK ODLG RQ WKH KRW FRDOV LV MHVXV
FKULVW LQ KLV SDVVLRQ, KLV ERGB “GHOLYHUHG IRU XV” RQ PRXQW FDOYDUB,
JLYHQ WR XV DOVR WR EH RXU IRRG LQ WKH EOHVVHG VDFUDPHQW ZKHUHEB “ZH VKRZ
WKH GHDWK RI WKH ORUG XQWLO KH FRPH.” WKH IDLWKIXO FDXJKW LQ WKH QHW RI
WKH FKXUFK PXVW EH EURXJKW WR WKDW EURLOHG ILVK (_SLVFLV DVVXV, FKULVWXV
SDVVXV_, VDBV VW. DXJXVWLQH), WKDW FUXFLILHG ORUG, DQG WKHB PXVW EH
LQFRUSRUDWHG ZLWK KLP EB SDUWDNLQJ RI WKH OLYLQJ EUHDG ZKLFK FDPH GRZQ
IURP KHDYHQ.

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _VDFULILFH RI LVDDF._]

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _UHVXUUHFWLRQ RI ODCDUXV._]

VXFK LV WKH IXOO PHDQLQJ RI WKH VFHQH DW WKH VHD RI WLEHULDV, DV
LQWHUSUHWHG DFFRUGLQJ WR WKH XQDQLPRXV FRQVHQW RI WKH IDWKHUV; DQG WKH
DGMXQFWV RI WKLV SLFWXUH VKRZ WKDW LW ZDV LQWHQGHG WR EH VR XQGHUVWRRG

GHVFULEHG; DQG RQ WKH RWKHU, WKH VDFULILFH RI LVDDF EB KLV IDWKHU, ZKLFK
ZDV VXUHOB D PRVW OLYHOB WBSH RI WKH VDFULILFH RI FKULVW XSRQ WKH DOWDU;
ZKHUHLQ EORRG LV QRW UHDOOB VKHG, EXW WKH ODPE LV RQOB “_DV LW ZHUH_
VODLQ,” MXVW DV LVDDF ZDV QRW UHDOOB VODLQ, EXW ZDV UHFHLYHG EDFN IURP
WKH GHDG, “IRU D SDUDEOH.” ODVWOB, DV KDV EHHQ PHQWLRQHG EHIRUH, WKHUH
IROORZV RQ WKH WKLUG ZDOO RI WKH VDPH FKDPEHU WKH QDWXUDO FRPSOHPHQW RI
WKH UHVW; WKH GRFWULQH RI WKH UHVXUUHFWLRQ, DV FRQWDLQHG LQ WKH IDFW
RI WKH ULVLQJ DJDLQ RI ODCDUXV. WKXV, WKLV ZKROH VHULHV RI SDLQWLQJV,
HAHFXWHG DW WKH HQG RI WKH VHFRQG FHQWXUB, RU ZLWKLQ WKH ILUVW WZHQWB RU
WKLUWB BHDUV RI WKH WKLUG, DQG UHSHDWHG (DV KDV EHHQ VDLG) LQ VHYHUDO
VXFFHVVLYH FKDPEHUV, ZDV D FRQWLQXDO KRPLOB, DV LW ZHUH, VHW EHIRUH WKH
HBHV RI WKH IDLWKIXO, LQ ZKLFK WKHB ZHUH UHPLQGHG RI WKH EHJLQQLQJ,
SURJUHVV, DQG FRQVXPPDWLRQ RI WKHLU QHZ DQG VXSHUQDWXUDO OLIH.

ZH GR QRW VDB WKDW HYHUB PRGHUQ FKULVWLDQ ZKR ORRNV DW WKHVH SDLQWLQJV
ZLOO WKXV UHDG WKHLU PHDQLQJ DW RQFH; EXW ZH EHOLHYH WKDW DOO DQFLHQW
FKULVWLDQV GLG VR, EHFDXVH LW LV FOHDU IURP WKH ZULWLQJV RI WKH DSRVWOHV
WKHPVHOYHV DQG WKHLU VXFFHVVRUV, WKDW QRWKLQJ ZDV PRUH IDPLOLDU WR WKH
FKULVWLDQ PLQG RI WKRVH GDBV WKDQ WKH VBPEROLFDO DQG SURSKHWLFDO PHDQLQJ
RI WKH IDFWV ERWK RI WKH ROG DQG RI WKH QHZ WHVWDPHQWV. WKHB EHOLHYHG
WKH IDFWV WKHPVHOYHV WR KDYH WDNHQ SODFH MXVW DV WKHB DUH UHFRUGHG, EXW
WKHB EHOLHYHG DOVR WKDW WKHB KDG D PBVWHULRXV VLJQLILFDWLRQ, ZKHUHEB
WKH WUXWKV RI WKH FKULVWLDQ IDLWK ZHUH LQVLQXDWHG RU HASUHVVHG, DQG
WKDW WKLV ZDV WKHLU KLJKHVW DQG WUXHVW PHDQLQJ. “SHUKDSV WKHUH LV QR RQH
UHFRUGHG PLUDFOH RI RXU ORUG,” VDBV VW. JUHJRUB, “ZKLFK LV QRW WKHUHIRUH
VHOHFWHG IRU UHFRUGLQJ EHFDXVH LW ZDV WKH WBSH RI VRPHWKLQJ WR KDSSHQ
LQ WKH FKXUFK;” DQG SUHFLVHOB WKH VDPH ZDV IHOW WR EH WUXH DOVR RI WKH
KLVWRULHV RI WKH SDWULDUFKDO DQG MHZLVK GLVSHQVDWLRQV. “DOO WKHVH WKLQJV
KDG KDSSHQHG WR WKHP LQ ILJXUH, DQG WKHB ZHUH ZULWWHQ IRU RXU FRUUHFWLRQ,
XSRQ ZKRP WKH HQGV RI WKH ZRUOG DUH FRPH.”

LW PDB QRW EH RIWHQ SRVVLEOH WR WUDFH DV FOHDUOB DV ZH KDYH MXVW GRQH
LQ D VLQJOH LQVWDQFH, WKH ORJLFDO RUGHU DQG GHSHQGHQFH RI WKH VHYHUDO
VXEMHFWV WKDW ZHUH VHOHFWHG IRU UHSUHVHQWDWLRQ LQ HDFK FKDPEHU RI WKH
FDWDFRPEV; WKHB PDB QRW DOZDBV KDYH EHHQ VR DGPLUDEOB DUUDQJHG DV
WR EH LQ IDFW HTXLYDOHQW, DV WKHVH ZHUH, WR D ZHOO-RUGHUHG GRJPDWLF
GLVFRXUVH. QHYHUWKHOHVV LW LV RQOB ZKHQ UHDG LQ WKLV ZDB, WKDW WKH
GHFRUDWLRQ RI WKH FDWDFRPEV FDQ EH PDGH WKRURXJKOB LQWHOOLJLEOH; DQG
LW LV FHUWDLQ WKDW VRPH VXFK PHDQLQJ PXVW KDYH EHHQ LQWHQGHG IURP WKH
ILUVW. WKH HAWUHPHOB OLPLWHG QXPEHU RI ELEOLFDO VXEMHFWV VHOHFWHG IRU
UHSUHVHQWDWLRQ, ZKLOH VXFK DQ LPPHQVH YDULHWB LV UHDOOB FRQWDLQHG LQ WKH
ELEOH (DQG VR PDQB RI WKRVH WKDW DUH QHJOHFWHG PLJKW KDYH VHHPHG HTXDOOB
VXLWDEOH IRU WKH SXUSRVH), DQG WKHQ DJDLQ, WKH WKRURXJKOB XQKLVWRULFDO
ZDB LQ ZKLFK WKHVH IHZ VXEMHFWV DUH GHDOW ZLWK, VKRZV FOHDUOB WKDW WKH
SULQFLSOH RI VHOHFWLRQ ZDV WKHRORJLFDO UDWKHU WKDQ DUWLVWLF. WKH DUWLVWV
ZHUH QRW OHIW WR LQGXOJH WKHLU RZQ XQIHWWHUHG IDQFB, EXW ZRUNHG XQGHU
HFFOHVLDVWLFDO VXSHUYLVLRQ; DQG WKH ELEOH VWRULHV ZKLFK WKHB GHSLFWHG
ZHUH QRW UHSUHVHQWHG DFFRUGLQJ WR WKHLU KLVWRULFDO YHULWB, EHFDXVH WKHB
ZHUH QRW LQWHQGHG WR EH D VRXYHQLU RI SDVW IDFWV, EXW WR VBPEROLVH DQG
VXJJHVW VRPHWKLQJ EHBRQG WKHPVHOYHV. LQ RUGHU, WKHUHIRUH, WR XQGHUVWDQG
WKHP, LW LV QHFHVVDUB WR EULQJ WKHP IDFH WR IDFH ZLWK WKH FKULVWLDQ
GRFWULQHV ZKLFK WKHB IRUHVKDGRZ.

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _QRH LQ WKH DUN._]

ORRN, IRU HADPSOH, DW WKH QXPHURXV SLFWXUHV RI QRH LQ WKH DUN ZKLFK
DSSHDU LQ WKH FDWDFRPEV, DOO UHVHPEOLQJ RQH DQRWKHU, EXW QRQH UHVHPEOLQJ
WKH UHDOLWB. LQVWHDG RI D YHVVHO, WKUHH VWRULHV KLJK, FRQWDLQLQJ HLJKW
KXPDQ EHLQJV DQG VSHFLPHQV RI HYHUB NLQG RI DQLPDO, ZH VHH RQOB D QDUURZ
ERA, EDUHOB ODUJH HQRXJK WR KROG RQH SHUVRQ, DQG WKDW SHUVRQ VRPHWLPHV D
ODGB, ZKRVH QDPH LV DOVR LQVFULEHG XSRQ LW SHUKDSV, EHLQJ WKH VDPH ODGB
(DV ZH OHDUQ IURP WKH LQVFULSWLRQ) ZKR OLHV EXULHG LQ WKH DGMDFHQW WRPE.
LI DOO DQFLHQW FKULVWLDQ OLWHUDWXUH KDG SHULVKHG, ZH VKRXOG KDYH EHHQ DW
D ORVV WR FRPSUHKHQG WKLV HQLJPD; EXW DV VRRQ DV ZH NQRZ WKDW WKH IDWKHUV
RI WKH FKXUFK VSHDN RI LW DV DQ DFNQRZOHGJHG IDFW, ZKLFK “QRERGB GRXEWV”
(WR XVH VW. DXJXVWLQH’V ZRUGV), WKDW WKH FKXUFK ZDV WBSLILHG EB WKH DUN,
D UDB RI OLJKW EHJLQV WR GDZQ XSRQ XV; DQG ZKHQ ZH FDOO WR PLQG WKDW
VW. SHWHU KLPVHOI VSHDNV RI WKH ZDWHUV RI EDSWLVP DV VDYLQJ PHQ’V VRXOV,
“HYHQ DV QRH DQG KLV IDPLOB ZHUH VDYHG EB WKH ZDWHUV RI WKH IORRG,” DOO
LV DW RQFH PDGH FOHDU. ZH VHH SODLQOB WKDW WKH IULHQGV RI WKH GHFHDVHG
KDYH LQWHQGHG WR VLJQLIB WKDW KH KDG EHHQ UHFHLYHG LQWR WKH DUN RI WKH
FKXUFK DQG PDGH D FKULVWLDQ EB EDSWLVP. DQG LI WKHB KDG DGGHG WR WKH
FRPSRVLWLRQ, DV WKHB RIWHQ GLG, WKH ILJXUH RI D GRYH EULQJLQJ DQ ROLYH
EUDQFK WR WKH SHUVRQ VWDQGLQJ LQ WKH DUN, WKLV DOVR HQWHUV LQWR WKH VDPH
LQWHUSUHWDWLRQ; LW ZDV VBPEROLFDO RI WKDW GLYLQH SHDFH ZKLFK FRPHV WR WKH
VRXO LQ WKLV ZRUOG EB IDLWK, DQG ZKLFK LV D SOHGJH RI WKH SHDFH JLYHQ EB
HYHUODVWLQJ KDSSLQHVV LQ WKH QHAW.

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _VFHQHV IURP WKH KLVWRUB RI MRQDV._]

WKH IUHTXHQW UHSHWLWLRQ RI WKH VWRUB RI MRQDV LQ D FKULVWLDQ FHPHWHUB
QHHGV QR HASODQDWLRQ, RXU ORUG KLPVHOI KDYLQJ SXW LW IRUZDUG DV D WBSH RI
KLV RZQ UHVXUUHFWLRQ, DQG VR D SOHGJH RI RXUV DOVR. WKH SDUWLFXODU IRUP,
KRZHYHU, XQGHU ZKLFK WKLV VWRUB DSSHDUV, ZDV QRW VXJJHVWHG, DV QRH’V DUN
ZDV, EB WKH SODFH ZKLFK LW KHOG LQ WKH FBFOH RI FKULVWLDQ GRFWULQH, EXW
UDWKHU EB D FHUWDLQ SDJDQ PRGHO ZLWK ZKLFK WKH URPDQV RI WKDW GDB ZHUH
YHUB IDPLOLDU. WKH PBWKRORJLFDO WDOH RI DQGURPHGD, DQG WKH VHD-PRQVWHU
WR ZKLFK VKH ZDV HASRVHG RQ WKH FRDVW QHDU MRSSD (IRU VR WKH VWRUB UDQ),
ZDV D IDYRXULWH VXEMHFW IRU WKH GHFRUDWLRQ RI WKH ZDOOV LQ URPDQ YLOODV,
WHPSOHV, DQG RWKHU SXEOLF EXLOGLQJV. LW PDB EH VHHQ LQ SRPSHLL, DQG,
PXFK QHDUHU WR WKH FDWDFRPEV, LQ URPH LWVHOI—_H.J._, LQ WKH EDUUDFNV RI
RQH RI WKH FRKRUWV RI WKH LPSHULDO SROLFH, GLVFRYHUHG D IHZ BHDUV DJR LQ
WUDVWHYHUH; DQG LQ ERWK SODFHV WKH PRQVWHU LV WKH SUHFLVH FRXQWHUSDUW
RI WKDW ZKLFK LV DOZDBV UHSUHVHQWHG DV VZDOORZLQJ RU FDVWLQJ XS MRQDV;
D NLQG RI GUDJRQ, ZLWK ODUJH KHDG DQG HDUV, D ORQJ VOHQGHU QHFN, DQG D
YHUB WRUWXRXV ERGB. RI FRXUVH, LQ WKH LQIDQFB RI FKULVWLDQ DUW, LW ZDV
FRQYHQLHQW WR KDYH D PRGHO DW KDQG WR UHSUHVHQW DQ XQNQRZQ PRQVWHU, DQG,
DV ZH KDYH VDLG, ZH GR QRW GRXEW WKDW WKLV LV WKH WUXH KLVWRUB RI LWV
RULJLQ. VWLOO WKLV ZDV QRW WKH RQOB UHDVRQ ZKLFK UHFRPPHQGHG WKH DGRSWLRQ
RI VR JURWHVTXH D IRUP; LW RIIHUHG WKH IXUWKHU DGYDQWDJH RI FUHDWLQJ DV
VWURQJ D FRQWUDVW DV SRVVLEOH EHWZHHQ WKLV “JUHDW ILVK,” ZKLFK ZDV D
WBSH RI GHDWK, DQG WKH RUGLQDUB ILVK, ZKLFK, DV ZH KDYH VHHQ, ZDV WKH
UHFRJQLVHG VBPERO RI WKH DXWKRU RI OLIH.

DQRWKHU LQFLGHQW LQ WKH OLIH RI MRQDV, ZKLFK ZDV RIWHQ SDLQWHG LQ WKH
FDWDFRPEV, ZDV KLV UHVWLQJ RQ WKH HDVW VLGH RI WKH FLWB RI QLQHYH,
XQGHU WKH VKDGH RI D FHUWDLQ SODQW ZKLFK JRG FDXVHG WR JURZ XS IRU KLV
SURWHFWLRQ, DQG ZKLFK KH DJDLQ FDXVHG DV VXGGHQOB WR ZLWKHU DZDB. LQ WKH
GDBV RI VW. MHURPH DQG VW. DXJXVWLQH WKHUH ZDV D GLVSXWH EHWZHHQ WKRVH
OHDUQHG GRFWRUV DV WR WKH SUHFLVH QDWXUH RI WKLV SODQW; DQG LQ WKH FRXUVH
RI LW VW. MHURPH DSSHDOHG WR WKHVH SDLQWLQJV DV EHDULQJ WHVWLPRQB LQ
IDYRXU RI KLV RZQ UHQGHULQJ RI WKH KHEUHZ ZRUG. ZH QHHG QRW HQWHU LQWR
WKH PHULWV RI WKH GLVSXWH, EXW LW LV LPSRUWDQW WR QRWH WKH IDFW RI WKH
DSSHDO, DV LW SHUHPSWRULOB UHIXWHV WKH ULGLFXORXV DVVHUWLRQV RI FHUWDLQ
DXWKRUV RI WKH SUHVHQW GDB, ZKR ZRXOG DVVLJQ YHUB UHFHQW GDWHV WR WKHVH
DQG VLPLODU SDLQWLQJV LQ WKH FDWDFRPEV. ZH NQRZ WKDW VW. MHURPH ZDV YHUB
IRQG, ZKHQ D ERB, RI YLVLWLQJ WKHVH SODFHV, DQG LW LV LQWHUHVWLQJ WR
KHDU KLP DSSHDOLQJ WR WKH SDLQWLQJV KH KDG VHHQ LQ WKHP DV WR “DQFLHQW
ZLWQHVVHV.” LW ZRXOG EH VWLOO PRUH LQWHUHVWLQJ, LI ZH FRXOG VDB ZLWK
FHUWDLQWB ZKDW ZHUH WKH PRWLYHV ZKLFK OHG WKH DQFLHQW FKULVWLDQV WR
FKRRVH WKLV VXEMHFW IRU VXFK IUHTXHQW FRQWHPSODWLRQ; ZKHWKHU WKHB UHDG
LQ LW RQOB D YHUB VWULNLQJ OHVVRQ DV WR WKH ZDWFKIXOQHVV RI GLYLQH
SURYLGHQFH, RU ZKHWKHU LW KDG D PRUH VXEWOH PHDQLQJ, DV D WBSH RI WKH
PHUFB RI JRG ZKLFK RYHUVKDGRZV WKH VRXOV RI WKH IDLWKIXO LQ WKH ORQJ
VOHHS RI GHDWK ZKLFK JRHV EHIRUH WKH VXQ RI WKH UHVXUUHFWLRQ. EXW ZKHUH
QR FOXH LV VXSSOLHG EB WKH ZULWLQJV RI FRWHPSRUDUB, RU QHDUOB FRWHPSRUDUB
DXWKRUV, ZH SUHIHU WR NHHS VLOHQFH UDWKHU WKDQ WR LQVLVW RQ DQB GRXEWIXO
LQWHUSUHWDWLRQ. DOO WKDW QHHG EH VDLG LV WKDW VXFK D SDLQWLQJ ZDV
FHUWDLQOB QRW RXW RI SODFH LQ D FKULVWLDQ FKXUFK RU FHPHWHUB, DQB PRUH
WKDQ WKH VWRUB RI DGDP DQG HYH, RU DQB RWKHU ELEOLFDO QDUUDWLYH ZKLFK
KDV UHIHUHQFH WR WKH GRFWULQHV RU SURPLVHV DQQRXQFHG EB FKULVWLDQLWB WR
WKH ZRUOG.

ZH GR QRW SUHWHQG WR HQXPHUDWH KHUH DOO WKH VXEMHFWV IURP WKH ROG DQG
QHZ WHVWDPHQWV WKDW ZHUH SDLQWHG LQ WKH FDWDFRPEV. ZH DUH EXW QDPLQJ
WKRVH WKDW ZHUH XVHG PRVW IUHTXHQWOB, WKDW VHHP PRVW LQWHUHVWLQJ, RU
ZKRVH VLJQLILFDWLRQ FDQ EH PRVW SUHFLVHOB GHWHUPLQHG. WKRVH ZKR KDYH VHHQ
WKH FDWDFRPEV WKHPVHOYHV ZLOO FDOO WR PLQG RWKHUV RI ZKLFK ZH KDYH QRW
VSRNHQ, EXW ZH WKLQN WKHLU PHDQLQJ LV JHQHUDOOB REYLRXV VR DV WR QHHG QR
HASODQDWLRQ. ZH ZLOO QDPH RQH FODVV RQOB RI WKHVH SDLQWLQJV; WKRVH LQ
ZKLFK RXU ORUG DQG KLV EOHVVHG PRWKHU DSSHDU. RXU UHDGHUV ZLOO KDUGOB
HASHFW WR ILQG DQBWKLQJ WKDW SUHWHQGV WR EH D SRUWUDLW RI HLWKHU RQH RU
WKH RWKHU. ZH KDYH VHHQ WKDW WKH GLVSRVLWLRQ LQ SULPLWLYH FKULVWLDQ DUW
ZDV WR UHSUHVHQW IDFWV UDWKHU WKDQ SHUVRQV, DQG WKH PBVWHUB ZKLFK WKH
IDFWV VLJQLILHG UDWKHU WKDQ WKH IDFWV WKHPVHOYHV. FKULVW, WKHUHIRUH,
DSSHDUV PRVW FRPPRQOB LQ WKH WBSLFDO FKDUDFWHU RI WKH JRRG VKHSKHUG, DQG
DV VXFK LV UHSUHVHQWHG LQ DSSURSULDWH IRUP DQG ZLWK VXLWDEOH DFFHVVRULHV,
RU KH VLWV LQ WKH PLGVW RI KLV DSRVWOHV, ZLWK D FKHVW RI YROXPHV DW KLV
IHHW, DV WKH JUHDW WHDFKHU RI WKH ZRUOG. RQFH, LQGHHG, KLV KHDG DQG EXVW
IRUP D PHGDOOLRQ RFFXSBLQJ WKH FHQWUH RI D URRI LQ D FKDPEHU RI WKH
FHPHWHUB RI VW. GRPLWLOOD, WKH VDPH LQ ZKLFK DSSHDU RUSKHXV DQG KLV OBUH.
LW LV D ZRUN RI WKH WKLUG FHQWXUB; WKHUH LV PRUH HYLGHQFH RI DQ LQWHQWLRQ
WR JLYH D GHILQLWH LQGLYLGXDO WBSH RI FRXQWHQDQFH, QHLWKHU LV WKH WBSH
DOWRJHWKHU XQOLNH WKDW ZKLFK WKH SUDFWLFH RI ODWHU DJHV KDV FRQVHFUDWHG
EB WUDGLWLRQDO XVDJH. QHYHUWKHOHVV RWKHUV RI WKH IRXUWK FHQWXUB DUH
HYLGHQWOB QRW FRSLHV RI WKH VDPH PRGHO, VR WKDW LW LV FOHDU WKDW LQ WKRVH
HDUOB GDBV WKHUH ZDV QR XQLIRUP DJUHHPHQW XSRQ WKH VXEMHFW.

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _WKH E. YLUJLQ DQG LVDLDV, IURP FHPHWHUB RI VW.
SULVFLOOD._]

RXU EOHVVHG ODGB DSSHDUV SULQFLSDOOB LQ WKH VFHQH RI WKH DGRUDWLRQ RI WKH
PDJL. WZR, WKUHH, RU IRXU RI WKHVH PHQ (DFFRUGLQJ WR WKH DUUDQJHPHQW RI
WKH JURXS DQG WKH VSDFH DW WKH DUWLVW’V GLVSRVDO) VWDQG LQ WKHLU RULHQWDO
GUHVV, SUHVHQWLQJ WKHLU JLIWV WR FKULVW ZKR VLWV RQ PDUB’V NQHH. RQFH RU
WZLFH DOVR WKH KROB FKLOG DSSHDUV LQ KLV PRWKHU’V DUPV, RU EHIRUH KHU
EUHDVW, ZLWKRXW UHIHUHQFH DSSDUHQWOB WR DQB SDUWLFXODU HYHQW LQ WKHLU
OLYHV, EXW HLWKHU DEVROXWHOB DORQH, RU VWDQGLQJ RSSRVLWH WR LVDLDV, DV
WKRXJK SUHVHQWLQJ LQ WKHPVHOYHV WKH IXOILOPHQW RI KLV SURSKHFLHV. RQH
RI WKHVH SDLQWLQJV LQ WKH FDWDFRPE RQ WKH YLD QRPHQWDQD EHORQJV WR WKH
IRXUWK FHQWXUB; EXW IRU DQRWKHU RI IDU KLJKHU DUWLVWLF PHULW, WR EH
VHHQ LQ WKH FDWDFRPE RI VW. SULVFLOOD, WKH PRVW FRPSHWHQW MXGJHV GR QRW
KHVLWDWH WR FODLP DOPRVW DSRVWROLF DQWLTXLWB; DQG WKH FODLP LV VXSSRUWHG
EB PDQB DQG ZHLJKWB DUJXPHQWV. ZH FDQQRW, KRZHYHU, GLVFXVV WKHP KHUH, IRU
ZH KDYH DOUHDGB HAFHHGHG WKH OLPLWV ZH KDG SURSRVHG WR RXUVHOYHV.

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _WKH E. YLUJLQ DQG PDJL._]

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _WKH E. YLUJLQ, IURP WKH FHPHWHUB RQ YLD QRPHQWDQD._]

LQ FRQFOXVLRQ, ZH ZLOO JLYH D VOLJKW VNHWFK RI WKH VXFFHVVLYH SKDVHV LQ
WKH GHYHORSPHQW RI FKULVWLDQ DUW ZLWKLQ WKH OLPLWV RI WKH ILUVW WKUHH
FHQWXULHV; IRU, WKDQNV WR GH URVVL’V DOPRVW PLFURVFRSLF HADPLQDWLRQ RI
HYHUB DFFHVVLEOH FRUQHU RI VXEWHUUDQHDQ URPH, HYHQ WKLV LV QRZ SRVVLEOH.
DV HDFK RI WKHVH SKDVHV ZDV GHULYHG IURP LWV SUHGHFHVVRU EB D QDWXUDO
VHTXHQFH RI LGHDV, LW LV QRW SUHWHQGHG WKDW WKHB DUH VHSDUDWHG IURP RQH
DQRWKHU EB VWULFW FKURQRORJLFDO ERXQGDULHV ZKLFK DUH QHYHU WUDQVJUHVVHG;
BHW WKH FKDUDFWHULVWLFV RI WKH VHYHUDO SHULRGV DUH, LQ WKH PDLQ,
VXIILFLHQWOB GLVWLQFW WR DOORZ RI WKHLU EHLQJ IROORZHG DV VDIH JXLGHV LQ
GHWHUPLQLQJ, DW OHDVW DSSURALPDWHOB, WKH DJH RI DQB SDUWLFXODU FODVV, RU
HYHQ LQGLYLGXDO VSHFLPHQ RI RUQDPHQWDWLRQ.

ZH KDYH DOUHDGB VHHQ WKDW SULPLWLYH FKULVWLDQ DUW VSUXQJ RXW RI DQ
DOOLDQFH RI DQFLHQW IRUPV ZLWK QHZ LGHDV; LQ LWV RXWZDUG SKBVLRJQRPB LW
SURFHHGHG GLUHFWOB, LQ SRLQW RI VWBOH DQG PHWKRG RI HAHFXWLRQ, IURP WKH
VFKRRO RI SDJDQ GHFRUDWLYH DUW, EXW LW ZDV DQLPDWHG EB D QHZ OLIH; DQG
WKHUHIRUH LW EHJDQ DW RQFH WR FUHDWH D SLFWRULDO FBFOH IRU LWVHOI, WDNHQ
SDUWOB IURP KLVWRULFDO DQG SDUWOB IURP DOOHJRULFDO PDWHULDOV. DW ILUVW
WKH DOOHJRULFDO HOHPHQW JUHDWOB SUHGRPLQDWHG. WKH ILVK DQG WKH DQFKRU,
WKH ODPE DQG WKH GRYH, WKH VKHSKHUG DQG WKH ILVKHUPDQ, PDB EH QDPHG DV
WKH PRVW SURPLQHQW HADPSOHV; DQG DOO WKHVH GXULQJ WKH ILUVW, RU, DV LW
KDV EHHQ VWBOHG, WKH KLHURJOBSKLF RU LGHRJUDSKLF SHULRG RI FKULVWLDQ
DUW, ZHUH FKDUDFWHULVHG EB WKH XWPRVW VLPSOLFLWB. WKH SULQFLSDO ILJXUH
XVXDOOB VWRRG DORQH; WKH ILVKHUPDQ LV FDWFKLQJ D ILVK, RU WKH VKHSKHUG LV
FDUUBLQJ D VKHHS XSRQ KLV VKRXOGHUV, DQG QRWKLQJ PRUH.

LQ WKH VHFRQG SHULRG—_L.H._, IURP WKH PLGGOH RI WKH VHFRQG WR WKH PLGGOH
RI WKH WKLUG FHQWXUB—WKH JRRG VKHSKHUG RFFXUV OHVV IUHTXHQWOB, DQG
LV UHSUHVHQWHG OHVV VLPSOB; KH FDUULHV D JRDW, RU KH SODBV KLV SLSH;
KH VWDQGV DPLG WUHHV LQ D JDUGHQ, RU LQ WKH PLGVW RI KLV IORFN, DQG
WKH VHYHUDO PHPEHUV RI KLV IORFN VWDQG LQ GLIIHUHQW DWWLWXGHV WRZDUGV
KLP, PDUNLQJ D GLIIHUHQFH RI LQWHUQDO GLVSRVLWLRQ. RWKHU ILJXUHV
DOVR XQGHUJR VLPLODU FKDQJHV; GLIIHUHQW HPEOHPV RU GLIIHUHQW WBSLFDO
KLVWRULHV DUH EOHQGHG WRJHWKHU, DQG WKH UHVXOW LV PRUH DUWLVWLF; D
PRUH EULOOLDQW WUDQVODWLRQ, VR WR VSHDN, LV WKXV JLYHQ RI WKH VDPH
WKRXJKWV DQG LGHDV ZLWK ZKLFK ZH KDYH EHHQ IDPLOLDU LQ D PRUH HOHPHQWDUB
IRUP IURP WKH EHJLQQLQJ. WKLV FKDQJH, RU UDWKHU WKLV JURZWK, ZDV LQ
WUXWK RQOB WKH QDWXUDO UHVXOW RI WLPH DQG RI WKH SLRXV PHGLWDWLRQ RI
VXFFHVVLYH JHQHUDWLRQV RI FKULVWLDQV HAHUFLVHG XSRQ WKH KLVWRUB RI WKHLU
IDLWK DQG XSRQ WKH RXWZDUG UHSUHVHQWDWLRQV RI LWV PBVWHULHV, LQ ZKLFK
WKHLU IRUHIDWKHUV KDG DOZDBV GHOLJKWHG. WKH EXG KDG HASDQGHG, DQG
WKH IXOO-EORZQ IORZHU GLVSODBHG QHZ EHDXWLHV—EHDXWLHV ZKLFK KDG EHHQ
WKHUH LQGHHG EHIRUH, EXW XQVHHQ. WKXV ZH PHHW DJDLQ ZLWK WKH DSRVWROLF
ILVKHUPDQ, EXW WKH ULYHU LQ ZKLFK KH ILVKHV LV QRZ D PBVWLFDO ULYHU,
IRUPHG EB WKH ZDWHUV ZKLFK KDYH IORZHG IURP WKH URFN VWUXFN EB PRVHV.
PRUH ELEOH KLVWRULHV DUH PDGH XVH RI; RU, LI QRW QRZ LQWURGXFHG IRU WKH
ILUVW WLPH, DUH XVHG PRUH IUHTXHQWOB—WKH KLVWRUB RI GDQLHO DQG RI MRQDV,
WKH VDFULILFH RI DEUDKDP, WKH UHVXUUHFWLRQ RI ODCDUXV, WKH KHDOLQJ RI
WKH SDUDOBWLF DW EHWKVDLGD, DQG RWKHUV. DQG DV DOO WKHVH KLVWRULHV KDYH
EHHQ LOOXVWUDWHG LQ WKH ZULWLQJV RI FRWHPSRUDUB IDWKHUV, WKH PRQXPHQWV
ZKLFK UHSUHVHQW WKHP DUH RI WKH KLJKHVW YDOXH DV DQ KLVWRULFDO HASUHVVLRQ
RI ZKDW FKULVWLDQV LQ WKRVH GDBV EHOLHYHG DQG WDXJKW. ERWK WKH ZULWLQJV
DQG WKH SDLQWLQJV DUH HYLGHQWOB WKH IDLWKIXO HFKR RI WKH VDPH GRFWULQDO
WHDFKLQJ DQG WUDGLWLRQ.

[LOOXVWUDWLRQ: _JODVV IURP WKH FDWDFRPEV, QRZ LQ YDWLFDQ OLEUDUB._]

WKHQ IROORZV D WKLUG SHULRG LQ WKH KLVWRUB RI FKULVWLDQ DUW, ZKLFK, LI
WKH ILUVW WZR KDYH EHHQ MXVWOB FRPSDUHG WR LWV VSULQJ DQG VXPPHU, PDB
LWVHOI EH FHUWDLQOB FDOOHG LWV DXWXPQ. LW HAWHQGV IURP WKH PLGGOH RI WKH
WKLUG FHQWXUB WR WKH DJH RI FRQVWDQWLQH; DQG GXULQJ WKLV SHULRG WKHUH LV
D FHUWDLQ IDOOLQJ RII RI OHDYHV, DFFRPSDQLHG EB D IXUWKHU GHYHORSPHQW RI
WKH IORZHU, ZLWKRXW, KRZHYHU, DQB DGGLWLRQ WR LWV EHDXWB. WKH VBPEROLFDO
HOHPHQW LV VHQVLEOB GLPLQLVKHG; ZKDW ZH KDYH YHQWXUHG WR FDOO FKULVWLDQ
KLHURJOBSKLFV DUH DOPRVW RU TXLWH DEDQGRQHG; WKH SDUDEOHV DOVR DUH OHVV
XVHG, DQG HYHQ WKH KLVWRULFDO WBSHV DUH UHSUHVHQWHG LQ D PRUH KDUG DQG
OLWHUDO IRUP. LI PRVHV LV VWLOO VHHQ VWULNLQJ WKH PBVWLFDO URFN, WKH
OLWHUDO RU KLVWRULFDO PRVHV LV DW KLV VLGH, WDNLQJ RII KLV VKRHV EHIRUH
GUDZLQJ QHDU WR WKH EXUQLQJ EXVK; RU WKH MHZV DUH WKHUH, LQ WKHLU ORZ
URXQG FDSV, GULQNLQJ RI WKH ZDWHUV; RU LI LW LV GHVLUHG WR NHHS WKH
PBVWLFDO VHQVH RI WKH KLVWRUB EHIRUH WKH SHRSOH, LW LV GHHPHG QHFHVVDUB
WR LQVFULEH WKH QDPH RI SHWUXV RYHU WKH KHDG RI PRVHV, DV ZH VHH LQ
WZR RU WKUHH VSHFLPHQV RI WKH JLOGHG JODVVHV IRXQG LQ WKH FDWDFRPEV,
DQG EHORQJLQJ SUREDEOB WR WKH IRXUWK FHQWXUB. FKULVW QR ORQJHU DSSHDUV
DV WKH JRRG VKHSKHUG, EXW VLWV RU VWDQGV LQ WKH PLGVW RI KLV DSRVWOHV,
RU, VWLOO PRUH IUHTXHQWOB, PLUDFXORXVOB PXOWLSOLHV WKH ORDYHV DQG
ILVKHV. WKH ILVK LV QR ORQJHU WKH PBVWLFDO PRQRJUDP, “FRQWDLQLQJ D
PXOWLWXGH RI PBVWHULHV,” EXW DSSHDUV RQOB DV D QHFHVVDUB IHDWXUH LQ WKH
UHSUHVHQWDWLRQ RI WKLV VDPH PLUDFOH. ODCDUXV DSSHDUV VZDWKHG OLNH D
PXPPB, LQ DFFRUGDQFH, DV ZH NQRZ, ZLWK WKH IDFW; EXW HDUOLHU DUWLVWV KDG
LGHDOLVHG KLP, DQG PDGH KLP ULVH IURP WKH WRPE BRXQJ, IUHH, DQG DFWLYH.
WKH WKUHH FKLOGUHQ UHIXVLQJ WR DGRUH WKH LPDJH VHW XS EB QDEXFKRGRQRVRU
DUH EURXJKW IRUZDUG, DQG SODFHG LQ MXAWDSRVLWLRQ ZLWK WKH WKUHH ZLVH PHQ
DGRULQJ WKH LQIDQW MHVXV, VXJJHVWLQJ D FRPSDULVRQ, RU UDWKHU D FRQWUDVW,
YHUB VXLWDEOH WR WKH DOWHUHG FLUFXPVWDQFHV RI WKH WLPHV.

RI WKHVH, RQOB RQH EHORQJV WR WKH ILUVW FHQWXUB, WZR WR WKH VHFRQG, WKH
WKLUG VXSSOLHV WZHQWB, DQG WKH IRXUWK DQG ILIWK DERXW ILYH KXQGUHG HDFK.

ILUVW, WKHQ, GH URVVL REVHUYHV LW DV D QRWDEOH IDFW, DWWHVWHG EB WKH

XUJHQW UHDVRQV IRU FKDQJLQJ RU RPLWWLQJ ZKDW WKH SDJDQV KDG EHHQ ZRQW WR
XVH; EXW WKH FKXUFK GLG QRW DW RQFH SURYLGH DQBWKLQJ HOVH LQ LWV VWHDG.
KHQFH WKH YHUB HDUOLHVW FKULVWLDQ WRPEVWRQHV RQOB UHFRUGHG WKH EDUH QDPH
RU QDPHV RI WKH GHFHDVHG, WR ZKLFK, LQ D _YHUB IHZ_ LQVWDQFHV, FKLHIOB

FDQQRW VWXGB D GRCHQ PRQXPHQWV RI SDJDQ URPH ZLWKRXW FRPLQJ DFURVV VRPH

DQG VODYHV. BHW LQ D QXPEHU RI FKULVWLDQ LQVFULSWLRQV LQ URPH, HAFHHGLQJ

WKH JRG ZKRP WKHB VHUYHG WKHUH ZDV QR UHVSHFW RI SHUVRQV; QHLWKHU GLG

IURP ERQGDJH, WR VRPH HDUWKOB PDVWHU, EHFDXVH WKHB WKRXJKW RQOB RI WKDW

RI WKH ORUG; DQG OLNHZLVH KH WKDW ZDV FDOOHG, EHLQJ IUHH, ZDV VWLOO WKH
ERQGPDQ RI FKULVW.”

ZH UHSHDW, WKHQ, WKDW WKH PRVW DQFLHQW LQVFULSWLRQV RQ FKULVWLDQ
JUDYHVWRQHV LQ URPH FRQVLVWHG PHUHOB RI WKH QDPH RI WKH GHFHDVHG;

D PRWLYH RI YDQLWB, EXW PHUHOB IRU WKH SXUSRVH RI LGHQWLILFDWLRQ.
ODUJH JURXSV RI LQVFULSWLRQV RI WKLV NLQG PDB VWLOO EH VHHQ LQ VRPH RI
WKH ROGHVW SRUWLRQV RI VXEWHUUDQHDQ URPH; WUDFHG LQ YHUPLOLRQ RQ WKH
WLOHV, DV LQ WKH FDWDFRPE RI VWD. SULVFLOOD, RU HQJUDYHG LQ OHWWHUV RI

PHQWLRQ LV QRZ PDGH RI WKH HADFW DJH RI WKH GHFHDVHG, DQG RI WKH OHQJWK
RI KLV PDUULHG OLIH, QRW DV WR BHDUV RQOB, EXW DV WR PRQWKV, DQG
VRPHWLPHV HYHQ DV WR GDBV DQG KRXUV; RI WKH GDB RI KLV GHDWK DOVR, PRUH

GDB RI WKH EXULDO (_GHSRVLWLR_) ZDV FUHHSLQJ LQWR XVH EHIRUH WKH HQG
RI WKH WKLUG FHQWXUB; IURP WKH PLGGOH RI WKH IRXUWK, LW EHFDPH OLWWOH

            *** HQG RI WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ HERRN D YLVLW WR WKH URPDQ FDWDFRPEV ***
        

    

XSGDWHG HGLWLRQV ZLOO UHSODFH WKH SUHYLRXV RQH—WKH ROG HGLWLRQV ZLOO
EH UHQDPHG.

FUHDWLQJ WKH ZRUNV IURP SULQW HGLWLRQV QRW SURWHFWHG EB X.V. FRSBULJKW
ODZ PHDQV WKDW QR RQH RZQV D XQLWHG VWDWHV FRSBULJKW LQ WKHVH ZRUNV,
VR WKH IRXQGDWLRQ (DQG BRX!) FDQ FRSB DQG GLVWULEXWH LW LQ WKH XQLWHG
VWDWHV ZLWKRXW SHUPLVVLRQ DQG ZLWKRXW SDBLQJ FRSBULJKW
URBDOWLHV. VSHFLDO UXOHV, VHW IRUWK LQ WKH JHQHUDO WHUPV RI XVH SDUW
RI WKLV OLFHQVH, DSSOB WR FRSBLQJ DQG GLVWULEXWLQJ SURMHFW
JXWHQEHUJ™ HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV WR SURWHFW WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™
FRQFHSW DQG WUDGHPDUN. SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ LV D UHJLVWHUHG WUDGHPDUN,
DQG PDB QRW EH XVHG LI BRX FKDUJH IRU DQ HERRN, HAFHSW EB IROORZLQJ
WKH WHUPV RI WKH WUDGHPDUN OLFHQVH, LQFOXGLQJ SDBLQJ URBDOWLHV IRU XVH
RI WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ WUDGHPDUN. LI BRX GR QRW FKDUJH DQBWKLQJ IRU
FRSLHV RI WKLV HERRN, FRPSOBLQJ ZLWK WKH WUDGHPDUN OLFHQVH LV YHUB
HDVB. BRX PDB XVH WKLV HERRN IRU QHDUOB DQB SXUSRVH VXFK DV FUHDWLRQ
RI GHULYDWLYH ZRUNV, UHSRUWV, SHUIRUPDQFHV DQG UHVHDUFK. SURMHFW
JXWHQEHUJ HERRNV PDB EH PRGLILHG DQG SULQWHG DQG JLYHQ DZDB—BRX PDB
GR SUDFWLFDOOB DQBWKLQJ LQ WKH XQLWHG VWDWHV ZLWK HERRNV QRW SURWHFWHG
EB X.V. FRSBULJKW ODZ. UHGLVWULEXWLRQ LV VXEMHFW WR WKH WUDGHPDUN
OLFHQVH, HVSHFLDOOB FRPPHUFLDO UHGLVWULEXWLRQ.


VWDUW: IXOO OLFHQVH

WKH IXOO SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ OLFHQVH

SOHDVH UHDG WKLV EHIRUH BRX GLVWULEXWH RU XVH WKLV ZRUN

WR SURWHFW WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ PLVVLRQ RI SURPRWLQJ WKH IUHH
GLVWULEXWLRQ RI HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV, EB XVLQJ RU GLVWULEXWLQJ WKLV ZRUN
(RU DQB RWKHU ZRUN DVVRFLDWHG LQ DQB ZDB ZLWK WKH SKUDVH “SURMHFW
JXWHQEHUJ”), BRX DJUHH WR FRPSOB ZLWK DOO WKH WHUPV RI WKH IXOO
SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ OLFHQVH DYDLODEOH ZLWK WKLV ILOH RU RQOLQH DW
ZZZ.JXWHQEHUJ.RUJ/OLFHQVH.

VHFWLRQ 1. JHQHUDO WHUPV RI XVH DQG UHGLVWULEXWLQJ SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™
HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV

1.D. EB UHDGLQJ RU XVLQJ DQB SDUW RI WKLV SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™
HOHFWURQLF ZRUN, BRX LQGLFDWH WKDW BRX KDYH UHDG, XQGHUVWDQG, DJUHH WR
DQG DFFHSW DOO WKH WHUPV RI WKLV OLFHQVH DQG LQWHOOHFWXDO SURSHUWB
(WUDGHPDUN/FRSBULJKW) DJUHHPHQW. LI BRX GR QRW DJUHH WR DELGH EB DOO
WKH WHUPV RI WKLV DJUHHPHQW, BRX PXVW FHDVH XVLQJ DQG UHWXUQ RU
GHVWURB DOO FRSLHV RI SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV LQ BRXU
SRVVHVVLRQ. LI BRX SDLG D IHH IRU REWDLQLQJ D FRSB RI RU DFFHVV WR D
SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ HOHFWURQLF ZRUN DQG BRX GR QRW DJUHH WR EH ERXQG
EB WKH WHUPV RI WKLV DJUHHPHQW, BRX PDB REWDLQ D UHIXQG IURP WKH SHUVRQ
RU HQWLWB WR ZKRP BRX SDLG WKH IHH DV VHW IRUWK LQ SDUDJUDSK 1.H.8.

1.E. “SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ” LV D UHJLVWHUHG WUDGHPDUN. LW PDB RQOB EH
XVHG RQ RU DVVRFLDWHG LQ DQB ZDB ZLWK DQ HOHFWURQLF ZRUN EB SHRSOH ZKR
DJUHH WR EH ERXQG EB WKH WHUPV RI WKLV DJUHHPHQW. WKHUH DUH D IHZ
WKLQJV WKDW BRX FDQ GR ZLWK PRVW SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV
HYHQ ZLWKRXW FRPSOBLQJ ZLWK WKH IXOO WHUPV RI WKLV DJUHHPHQW. VHH
SDUDJUDSK 1.F EHORZ. WKHUH DUH D ORW RI WKLQJV BRX FDQ GR ZLWK SURMHFW
JXWHQEHUJ™ HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV LI BRX IROORZ WKH WHUPV RI WKLV
DJUHHPHQW DQG KHOS SUHVHUYH IUHH IXWXUH DFFHVV WR SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™
HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV. VHH SDUDJUDSK 1.H EHORZ.

1.F. WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ OLWHUDUB DUFKLYH IRXQGDWLRQ (“WKH
IRXQGDWLRQ” RU SJODI), RZQV D FRPSLODWLRQ FRSBULJKW LQ WKH FROOHFWLRQ
RI SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV. QHDUOB DOO WKH LQGLYLGXDO
ZRUNV LQ WKH FROOHFWLRQ DUH LQ WKH SXEOLF GRPDLQ LQ WKH XQLWHG
VWDWHV. LI DQ LQGLYLGXDO ZRUN LV XQSURWHFWHG EB FRSBULJKW ODZ LQ WKH
XQLWHG VWDWHV DQG BRX DUH ORFDWHG LQ WKH XQLWHG VWDWHV, ZH GR QRW
FODLP D ULJKW WR SUHYHQW BRX IURP FRSBLQJ, GLVWULEXWLQJ, SHUIRUPLQJ,
GLVSODBLQJ RU FUHDWLQJ GHULYDWLYH ZRUNV EDVHG RQ WKH ZRUN DV ORQJ DV
DOO UHIHUHQFHV WR SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ DUH UHPRYHG. RI FRXUVH, ZH KRSH
WKDW BRX ZLOO VXSSRUW WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ PLVVLRQ RI SURPRWLQJ
IUHH DFFHVV WR HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV EB IUHHOB VKDULQJ SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™
ZRUNV LQ FRPSOLDQFH ZLWK WKH WHUPV RI WKLV DJUHHPHQW IRU NHHSLQJ WKH
SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ QDPH DVVRFLDWHG ZLWK WKH ZRUN. BRX FDQ HDVLOB
FRPSOB ZLWK WKH WHUPV RI WKLV DJUHHPHQW EB NHHSLQJ WKLV ZRUN LQ WKH
VDPH IRUPDW ZLWK LWV DWWDFKHG IXOO SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ OLFHQVH ZKHQ
BRX VKDUH LW ZLWKRXW FKDUJH ZLWK RWKHUV.

1.G. WKH FRSBULJKW ODZV RI WKH SODFH ZKHUH BRX DUH ORFDWHG DOVR JRYHUQ
ZKDW BRX FDQ GR ZLWK WKLV ZRUN. FRSBULJKW ODZV LQ PRVW FRXQWULHV DUH
LQ D FRQVWDQW VWDWH RI FKDQJH. LI BRX DUH RXWVLGH WKH XQLWHG VWDWHV,
FKHFN WKH ODZV RI BRXU FRXQWUB LQ DGGLWLRQ WR WKH WHUPV RI WKLV
DJUHHPHQW EHIRUH GRZQORDGLQJ, FRSBLQJ, GLVSODBLQJ, SHUIRUPLQJ,
GLVWULEXWLQJ RU FUHDWLQJ GHULYDWLYH ZRUNV EDVHG RQ WKLV ZRUN RU DQB
RWKHU SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ ZRUN. WKH IRXQGDWLRQ PDNHV QR
UHSUHVHQWDWLRQV FRQFHUQLQJ WKH FRSBULJKW VWDWXV RI DQB ZRUN LQ DQB
FRXQWUB RWKHU WKDQ WKH XQLWHG VWDWHV.

1.H. XQOHVV BRX KDYH UHPRYHG DOO UHIHUHQFHV WR SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ:

1.H.1. WKH IROORZLQJ VHQWHQFH, ZLWK DFWLYH OLQNV WR, RU RWKHU
LPPHGLDWH DFFHVV WR, WKH IXOO SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ OLFHQVH PXVW DSSHDU
SURPLQHQWOB ZKHQHYHU DQB FRSB RI D SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ ZRUN (DQB ZRUN
RQ ZKLFK WKH SKUDVH “SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ” DSSHDUV, RU ZLWK ZKLFK WKH
SKUDVH “SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ” LV DVVRFLDWHG) LV DFFHVVHG, GLVSODBHG,
SHUIRUPHG, YLHZHG, FRSLHG RU GLVWULEXWHG:

    WKLV HERRN LV IRU WKH XVH RI DQBRQH DQBZKHUH LQ WKH XQLWHG VWDWHV DQG PRVW
    RWKHU SDUWV RI WKH ZRUOG DW QR FRVW DQG ZLWK DOPRVW QR UHVWULFWLRQV
    ZKDWVRHYHU. BRX PDB FRSB LW, JLYH LW DZDB RU UH-XVH LW XQGHU WKH WHUPV
    RI WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ OLFHQVH LQFOXGHG ZLWK WKLV HERRN RU RQOLQH
    DW ZZZ.JXWHQEHUJ.RUJ. LI BRX
    DUH QRW ORFDWHG LQ WKH XQLWHG VWDWHV, BRX ZLOO KDYH WR FKHFN WKH ODZV
    RI WKH FRXQWUB ZKHUH BRX DUH ORFDWHG EHIRUH XVLQJ WKLV HERRN.
  
1.H.2. LI DQ LQGLYLGXDO SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ HOHFWURQLF ZRUN LV
GHULYHG IURP WHAWV QRW SURWHFWHG EB X.V. FRSBULJKW ODZ (GRHV QRW
FRQWDLQ D QRWLFH LQGLFDWLQJ WKDW LW LV SRVWHG ZLWK SHUPLVVLRQ RI WKH
FRSBULJKW KROGHU), WKH ZRUN FDQ EH FRSLHG DQG GLVWULEXWHG WR DQBRQH LQ
WKH XQLWHG VWDWHV ZLWKRXW SDBLQJ DQB IHHV RU FKDUJHV. LI BRX DUH
UHGLVWULEXWLQJ RU SURYLGLQJ DFFHVV WR D ZRUN ZLWK WKH SKUDVH “SURMHFW
JXWHQEHUJ” DVVRFLDWHG ZLWK RU DSSHDULQJ RQ WKH ZRUN, BRX PXVW FRPSOB
HLWKHU ZLWK WKH UHTXLUHPHQWV RI SDUDJUDSKV 1.H.1 WKURXJK 1.H.7 RU
REWDLQ SHUPLVVLRQ IRU WKH XVH RI WKH ZRUN DQG WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™
WUDGHPDUN DV VHW IRUWK LQ SDUDJUDSKV 1.H.8 RU 1.H.9.

1.H.3. LI DQ LQGLYLGXDO SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ HOHFWURQLF ZRUN LV SRVWHG
ZLWK WKH SHUPLVVLRQ RI WKH FRSBULJKW KROGHU, BRXU XVH DQG GLVWULEXWLRQ
PXVW FRPSOB ZLWK ERWK SDUDJUDSKV 1.H.1 WKURXJK 1.H.7 DQG DQB
DGGLWLRQDO WHUPV LPSRVHG EB WKH FRSBULJKW KROGHU. DGGLWLRQDO WHUPV
ZLOO EH OLQNHG WR WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ OLFHQVH IRU DOO ZRUNV
SRVWHG ZLWK WKH SHUPLVVLRQ RI WKH FRSBULJKW KROGHU IRXQG DW WKH
EHJLQQLQJ RI WKLV ZRUN.

1.H.4. GR QRW XQOLQN RU GHWDFK RU UHPRYH WKH IXOO SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™
OLFHQVH WHUPV IURP WKLV ZRUN, RU DQB ILOHV FRQWDLQLQJ D SDUW RI WKLV
ZRUN RU DQB RWKHU ZRUN DVVRFLDWHG ZLWK SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™.

1.H.5. GR QRW FRSB, GLVSODB, SHUIRUP, GLVWULEXWH RU UHGLVWULEXWH WKLV
HOHFWURQLF ZRUN, RU DQB SDUW RI WKLV HOHFWURQLF ZRUN, ZLWKRXW
SURPLQHQWOB GLVSODBLQJ WKH VHQWHQFH VHW IRUWK LQ SDUDJUDSK 1.H.1 ZLWK
DFWLYH OLQNV RU LPPHGLDWH DFFHVV WR WKH IXOO WHUPV RI WKH SURMHFW
JXWHQEHUJ™ OLFHQVH.

1.H.6. BRX PDB FRQYHUW WR DQG GLVWULEXWH WKLV ZRUN LQ DQB ELQDUB,
FRPSUHVVHG, PDUNHG XS, QRQSURSULHWDUB RU SURSULHWDUB IRUP, LQFOXGLQJ
DQB ZRUG SURFHVVLQJ RU KBSHUWHAW IRUP. KRZHYHU, LI BRX SURYLGH DFFHVV
WR RU GLVWULEXWH FRSLHV RI D SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ ZRUN LQ D IRUPDW
RWKHU WKDQ “SODLQ YDQLOOD DVFLL” RU RWKHU IRUPDW XVHG LQ WKH RIILFLDO
YHUVLRQ SRVWHG RQ WKH RIILFLDO SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ ZHEVLWH
(ZZZ.JXWHQEHUJ.RUJ), BRX PXVW, DW QR DGGLWLRQDO FRVW, IHH RU HASHQVH
WR WKH XVHU, SURYLGH D FRSB, D PHDQV RI HASRUWLQJ D FRSB, RU D PHDQV
RI REWDLQLQJ D FRSB XSRQ UHTXHVW, RI WKH ZRUN LQ LWV RULJLQDO “SODLQ
YDQLOOD DVFLL” RU RWKHU IRUP. DQB DOWHUQDWH IRUPDW PXVW LQFOXGH WKH
IXOO SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ OLFHQVH DV VSHFLILHG LQ SDUDJUDSK 1.H.1.

1.H.7. GR QRW FKDUJH D IHH IRU DFFHVV WR, YLHZLQJ, GLVSODBLQJ,
SHUIRUPLQJ, FRSBLQJ RU GLVWULEXWLQJ DQB SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ ZRUNV
XQOHVV BRX FRPSOB ZLWK SDUDJUDSK 1.H.8 RU 1.H.9.

1.H.8. BRX PDB FKDUJH D UHDVRQDEOH IHH IRU FRSLHV RI RU SURYLGLQJ
DFFHVV WR RU GLVWULEXWLQJ SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV
SURYLGHG WKDW:

    • BRX SDB D URBDOWB IHH RI 20% RI WKH JURVV SURILWV BRX GHULYH IURP
        WKH XVH RI SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ ZRUNV FDOFXODWHG XVLQJ WKH PHWKRG
        BRX DOUHDGB XVH WR FDOFXODWH BRXU DSSOLFDEOH WDAHV. WKH IHH LV RZHG
        WR WKH RZQHU RI WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ WUDGHPDUN, EXW KH KDV
        DJUHHG WR GRQDWH URBDOWLHV XQGHU WKLV SDUDJUDSK WR WKH SURMHFW
        JXWHQEHUJ OLWHUDUB DUFKLYH IRXQGDWLRQ. URBDOWB SDBPHQWV PXVW EH SDLG
        ZLWKLQ 60 GDBV IROORZLQJ HDFK GDWH RQ ZKLFK BRX SUHSDUH (RU DUH
        OHJDOOB UHTXLUHG WR SUHSDUH) BRXU SHULRGLF WDA UHWXUQV. URBDOWB
        SDBPHQWV VKRXOG EH FOHDUOB PDUNHG DV VXFK DQG VHQW WR WKH SURMHFW
        JXWHQEHUJ OLWHUDUB DUFKLYH IRXQGDWLRQ DW WKH DGGUHVV VSHFLILHG LQ
        VHFWLRQ 4, “LQIRUPDWLRQ DERXW GRQDWLRQV WR WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ
        OLWHUDUB DUFKLYH IRXQGDWLRQ.”
    
    • BRX SURYLGH D IXOO UHIXQG RI DQB PRQHB SDLG EB D XVHU ZKR QRWLILHV
        BRX LQ ZULWLQJ (RU EB H-PDLO) ZLWKLQ 30 GDBV RI UHFHLSW WKDW V/KH
        GRHV QRW DJUHH WR WKH WHUPV RI WKH IXOO SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™
        OLFHQVH. BRX PXVW UHTXLUH VXFK D XVHU WR UHWXUQ RU GHVWURB DOO
        FRSLHV RI WKH ZRUNV SRVVHVVHG LQ D SKBVLFDO PHGLXP DQG GLVFRQWLQXH
        DOO XVH RI DQG DOO DFFHVV WR RWKHU FRSLHV RI SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™
        ZRUNV.
    
    • BRX SURYLGH, LQ DFFRUGDQFH ZLWK SDUDJUDSK 1.I.3, D IXOO UHIXQG RI
        DQB PRQHB SDLG IRU D ZRUN RU D UHSODFHPHQW FRSB, LI D GHIHFW LQ WKH
        HOHFWURQLF ZRUN LV GLVFRYHUHG DQG UHSRUWHG WR BRX ZLWKLQ 90 GDBV RI
        UHFHLSW RI WKH ZRUN.
    
    • BRX FRPSOB ZLWK DOO RWKHU WHUPV RI WKLV DJUHHPHQW IRU IUHH
        GLVWULEXWLRQ RI SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ ZRUNV.
    

1.H.9. LI BRX ZLVK WR FKDUJH D IHH RU GLVWULEXWH D SURMHFW
JXWHQEHUJ™ HOHFWURQLF ZRUN RU JURXS RI ZRUNV RQ GLIIHUHQW WHUPV WKDQ
DUH VHW IRUWK LQ WKLV DJUHHPHQW, BRX PXVW REWDLQ SHUPLVVLRQ LQ ZULWLQJ
IURP WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ OLWHUDUB DUFKLYH IRXQGDWLRQ, WKH PDQDJHU RI
WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ WUDGHPDUN. FRQWDFW WKH IRXQGDWLRQ DV VHW
IRUWK LQ VHFWLRQ 3 EHORZ.

1.I.

1.I.1. SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ YROXQWHHUV DQG HPSORBHHV HASHQG FRQVLGHUDEOH
HIIRUW WR LGHQWLIB, GR FRSBULJKW UHVHDUFK RQ, WUDQVFULEH DQG SURRIUHDG
ZRUNV QRW SURWHFWHG EB X.V. FRSBULJKW ODZ LQ FUHDWLQJ WKH SURMHFW
JXWHQEHUJ™ FROOHFWLRQ. GHVSLWH WKHVH HIIRUWV, SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™
HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV, DQG WKH PHGLXP RQ ZKLFK WKHB PDB EH VWRUHG, PDB
FRQWDLQ “GHIHFWV,” VXFK DV, EXW QRW OLPLWHG WR, LQFRPSOHWH, LQDFFXUDWH
RU FRUUXSW GDWD, WUDQVFULSWLRQ HUURUV, D FRSBULJKW RU RWKHU
LQWHOOHFWXDO SURSHUWB LQIULQJHPHQW, D GHIHFWLYH RU GDPDJHG GLVN RU
RWKHU PHGLXP, D FRPSXWHU YLUXV, RU FRPSXWHU FRGHV WKDW GDPDJH RU
FDQQRW EH UHDG EB BRXU HTXLSPHQW.

1.I.2. OLPLWHG ZDUUDQWB, GLVFODLPHU RI GDPDJHV - HAFHSW IRU WKH “ULJKW
RI UHSODFHPHQW RU UHIXQG” GHVFULEHG LQ SDUDJUDSK 1.I.3, WKH SURMHFW
JXWHQEHUJ OLWHUDUB DUFKLYH IRXQGDWLRQ, WKH RZQHU RI WKH SURMHFW
JXWHQEHUJ™ WUDGHPDUN, DQG DQB RWKHU SDUWB GLVWULEXWLQJ D SURMHFW
JXWHQEHUJ™ HOHFWURQLF ZRUN XQGHU WKLV DJUHHPHQW, GLVFODLP DOO
OLDELOLWB WR BRX IRU GDPDJHV, FRVWV DQG HASHQVHV, LQFOXGLQJ OHJDO
IHHV. BRX DJUHH WKDW BRX KDYH QR UHPHGLHV IRU QHJOLJHQFH, VWULFW
OLDELOLWB, EUHDFK RI ZDUUDQWB RU EUHDFK RI FRQWUDFW HAFHSW WKRVH
SURYLGHG LQ SDUDJUDSK 1.I.3. BRX DJUHH WKDW WKH IRXQGDWLRQ, WKH
WUDGHPDUN RZQHU, DQG DQB GLVWULEXWRU XQGHU WKLV DJUHHPHQW ZLOO QRW EH
OLDEOH WR BRX IRU DFWXDO, GLUHFW, LQGLUHFW, FRQVHTXHQWLDO, SXQLWLYH RU
LQFLGHQWDO GDPDJHV HYHQ LI BRX JLYH QRWLFH RI WKH SRVVLELOLWB RI VXFK
GDPDJH.

1.I.3. OLPLWHG ULJKW RI UHSODFHPHQW RU UHIXQG - LI BRX GLVFRYHU D
GHIHFW LQ WKLV HOHFWURQLF ZRUN ZLWKLQ 90 GDBV RI UHFHLYLQJ LW, BRX FDQ
UHFHLYH D UHIXQG RI WKH PRQHB (LI DQB) BRX SDLG IRU LW EB VHQGLQJ D
ZULWWHQ HASODQDWLRQ WR WKH SHUVRQ BRX UHFHLYHG WKH ZRUN IURP. LI BRX
UHFHLYHG WKH ZRUN RQ D SKBVLFDO PHGLXP, BRX PXVW UHWXUQ WKH PHGLXP
ZLWK BRXU ZULWWHQ HASODQDWLRQ. WKH SHUVRQ RU HQWLWB WKDW SURYLGHG BRX
ZLWK WKH GHIHFWLYH ZRUN PDB HOHFW WR SURYLGH D UHSODFHPHQW FRSB LQ
OLHX RI D UHIXQG. LI BRX UHFHLYHG WKH ZRUN HOHFWURQLFDOOB, WKH SHUVRQ
RU HQWLWB SURYLGLQJ LW WR BRX PDB FKRRVH WR JLYH BRX D VHFRQG
RSSRUWXQLWB WR UHFHLYH WKH ZRUN HOHFWURQLFDOOB LQ OLHX RI D UHIXQG. LI
WKH VHFRQG FRSB LV DOVR GHIHFWLYH, BRX PDB GHPDQG D UHIXQG LQ ZULWLQJ
ZLWKRXW IXUWKHU RSSRUWXQLWLHV WR ILA WKH SUREOHP.

1.I.4. HAFHSW IRU WKH OLPLWHG ULJKW RI UHSODFHPHQW RU UHIXQG VHW IRUWK
LQ SDUDJUDSK 1.I.3, WKLV ZRUN LV SURYLGHG WR BRX ‘DV-LV’, ZLWK QR
RWKHU ZDUUDQWLHV RI DQB NLQG, HASUHVV RU LPSOLHG, LQFOXGLQJ EXW QRW
OLPLWHG WR ZDUUDQWLHV RI PHUFKDQWDELOLWB RU ILWQHVV IRU DQB SXUSRVH.

1.I.5. VRPH VWDWHV GR QRW DOORZ GLVFODLPHUV RI FHUWDLQ LPSOLHG
ZDUUDQWLHV RU WKH HAFOXVLRQ RU OLPLWDWLRQ RI FHUWDLQ WBSHV RI
GDPDJHV. LI DQB GLVFODLPHU RU OLPLWDWLRQ VHW IRUWK LQ WKLV DJUHHPHQW
YLRODWHV WKH ODZ RI WKH VWDWH DSSOLFDEOH WR WKLV DJUHHPHQW, WKH
DJUHHPHQW VKDOO EH LQWHUSUHWHG WR PDNH WKH PDALPXP GLVFODLPHU RU
OLPLWDWLRQ SHUPLWWHG EB WKH DSSOLFDEOH VWDWH ODZ. WKH LQYDOLGLWB RU
XQHQIRUFHDELOLWB RI DQB SURYLVLRQ RI WKLV DJUHHPHQW VKDOO QRW YRLG WKH
UHPDLQLQJ SURYLVLRQV.

1.I.6. LQGHPQLWB - BRX DJUHH WR LQGHPQLIB DQG KROG WKH IRXQGDWLRQ, WKH
WUDGHPDUN RZQHU, DQB DJHQW RU HPSORBHH RI WKH IRXQGDWLRQ, DQBRQH
SURYLGLQJ FRSLHV RI SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV LQ
DFFRUGDQFH ZLWK WKLV DJUHHPHQW, DQG DQB YROXQWHHUV DVVRFLDWHG ZLWK WKH
SURGXFWLRQ, SURPRWLRQ DQG GLVWULEXWLRQ RI SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™
HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV, KDUPOHVV IURP DOO OLDELOLWB, FRVWV DQG HASHQVHV,
LQFOXGLQJ OHJDO IHHV, WKDW DULVH GLUHFWOB RU LQGLUHFWOB IURP DQB RI
WKH IROORZLQJ ZKLFK BRX GR RU FDXVH WR RFFXU: (D) GLVWULEXWLRQ RI WKLV
RU DQB SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ ZRUN, (E) DOWHUDWLRQ, PRGLILFDWLRQ, RU
DGGLWLRQV RU GHOHWLRQV WR DQB SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ ZRUN, DQG (F) DQB
GHIHFW BRX FDXVH.

VHFWLRQ 2. LQIRUPDWLRQ DERXW WKH PLVVLRQ RI SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™

SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ LV VBQRQBPRXV ZLWK WKH IUHH GLVWULEXWLRQ RI
HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV LQ IRUPDWV UHDGDEOH EB WKH ZLGHVW YDULHWB RI
FRPSXWHUV LQFOXGLQJ REVROHWH, ROG, PLGGOH-DJHG DQG QHZ FRPSXWHUV. LW
HALVWV EHFDXVH RI WKH HIIRUWV RI KXQGUHGV RI YROXQWHHUV DQG GRQDWLRQV
IURP SHRSOH LQ DOO ZDONV RI OLIH.

YROXQWHHUV DQG ILQDQFLDO VXSSRUW WR SURYLGH YROXQWHHUV ZLWK WKH
DVVLVWDQFH WKHB QHHG DUH FULWLFDO WR UHDFKLQJ SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™’V
JRDOV DQG HQVXULQJ WKDW WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ FROOHFWLRQ ZLOO
UHPDLQ IUHHOB DYDLODEOH IRU JHQHUDWLRQV WR FRPH. LQ 2001, WKH SURMHFW
JXWHQEHUJ OLWHUDUB DUFKLYH IRXQGDWLRQ ZDV FUHDWHG WR SURYLGH D VHFXUH
DQG SHUPDQHQW IXWXUH IRU SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ DQG IXWXUH
JHQHUDWLRQV. WR OHDUQ PRUH DERXW WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ OLWHUDUB
DUFKLYH IRXQGDWLRQ DQG KRZ BRXU HIIRUWV DQG GRQDWLRQV FDQ KHOS, VHH
VHFWLRQV 3 DQG 4 DQG WKH IRXQGDWLRQ LQIRUPDWLRQ SDJH DW ZZZ.JXWHQEHUJ.RUJ.

VHFWLRQ 3. LQIRUPDWLRQ DERXW WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ OLWHUDUB DUFKLYH IRXQGDWLRQ

WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ OLWHUDUB DUFKLYH IRXQGDWLRQ LV D QRQ-SURILW
501(F)(3) HGXFDWLRQDO FRUSRUDWLRQ RUJDQLCHG XQGHU WKH ODZV RI WKH
VWDWH RI PLVVLVVLSSL DQG JUDQWHG WDA HAHPSW VWDWXV EB WKH LQWHUQDO
UHYHQXH VHUYLFH. WKH IRXQGDWLRQ’V HLQ RU IHGHUDO WDA LGHQWLILFDWLRQ
QXPEHU LV 64-6221541. FRQWULEXWLRQV WR WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ OLWHUDUB
DUFKLYH IRXQGDWLRQ DUH WDA GHGXFWLEOH WR WKH IXOO HAWHQW SHUPLWWHG EB
X.V. IHGHUDO ODZV DQG BRXU VWDWH’V ODZV.

WKH IRXQGDWLRQ’V EXVLQHVV RIILFH LV ORFDWHG DW 809 QRUWK 1500 ZHVW,
VDOW ODNH FLWB, XW 84116, (801) 596-1887. HPDLO FRQWDFW OLQNV DQG XS
WR GDWH FRQWDFW LQIRUPDWLRQ FDQ EH IRXQG DW WKH IRXQGDWLRQ’V ZHEVLWH
DQG RIILFLDO SDJH DW ZZZ.JXWHQEHUJ.RUJ/FRQWDFW

VHFWLRQ 4. LQIRUPDWLRQ DERXW GRQDWLRQV WR WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ
OLWHUDUB DUFKLYH IRXQGDWLRQ

SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ GHSHQGV XSRQ DQG FDQQRW VXUYLYH ZLWKRXW ZLGHVSUHDG
SXEOLF VXSSRUW DQG GRQDWLRQV WR FDUUB RXW LWV PLVVLRQ RI
LQFUHDVLQJ WKH QXPEHU RI SXEOLF GRPDLQ DQG OLFHQVHG ZRUNV WKDW FDQ EH
IUHHOB GLVWULEXWHG LQ PDFKLQH-UHDGDEOH IRUP DFFHVVLEOH EB WKH ZLGHVW
DUUDB RI HTXLSPHQW LQFOXGLQJ RXWGDWHG HTXLSPHQW. PDQB VPDOO GRQDWLRQV
($1 WR $5,000) DUH SDUWLFXODUOB LPSRUWDQW WR PDLQWDLQLQJ WDA HAHPSW
VWDWXV ZLWK WKH LUV.

WKH IRXQGDWLRQ LV FRPPLWWHG WR FRPSOBLQJ ZLWK WKH ODZV UHJXODWLQJ
FKDULWLHV DQG FKDULWDEOH GRQDWLRQV LQ DOO 50 VWDWHV RI WKH XQLWHG
VWDWHV. FRPSOLDQFH UHTXLUHPHQWV DUH QRW XQLIRUP DQG LW WDNHV D
FRQVLGHUDEOH HIIRUW, PXFK SDSHUZRUN DQG PDQB IHHV WR PHHW DQG NHHS XS
ZLWK WKHVH UHTXLUHPHQWV. ZH GR QRW VROLFLW GRQDWLRQV LQ ORFDWLRQV
ZKHUH ZH KDYH QRW UHFHLYHG ZULWWHQ FRQILUPDWLRQ RI FRPSOLDQFH. WR VHQG
GRQDWLRQV RU GHWHUPLQH WKH VWDWXV RI FRPSOLDQFH IRU DQB SDUWLFXODU VWDWH
YLVLW ZZZ.JXWHQEHUJ.RUJ/GRQDWH.

ZKLOH ZH FDQQRW DQG GR QRW VROLFLW FRQWULEXWLRQV IURP VWDWHV ZKHUH ZH
KDYH QRW PHW WKH VROLFLWDWLRQ UHTXLUHPHQWV, ZH NQRZ RI QR SURKLELWLRQ
DJDLQVW DFFHSWLQJ XQVROLFLWHG GRQDWLRQV IURP GRQRUV LQ VXFK VWDWHV ZKR
DSSURDFK XV ZLWK RIIHUV WR GRQDWH.

LQWHUQDWLRQDO GRQDWLRQV DUH JUDWHIXOOB DFFHSWHG, EXW ZH FDQQRW PDNH
DQB VWDWHPHQWV FRQFHUQLQJ WDA WUHDWPHQW RI GRQDWLRQV UHFHLYHG IURP
RXWVLGH WKH XQLWHG VWDWHV. X.V. ODZV DORQH VZDPS RXU VPDOO VWDII.

SOHDVH FKHFN WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ ZHE SDJHV IRU FXUUHQW GRQDWLRQ
PHWKRGV DQG DGGUHVVHV. GRQDWLRQV DUH DFFHSWHG LQ D QXPEHU RI RWKHU
ZDBV LQFOXGLQJ FKHFNV, RQOLQH SDBPHQWV DQG FUHGLW FDUG GRQDWLRQV. WR
GRQDWH, SOHDVH YLVLW: ZZZ.JXWHQEHUJ.RUJ/GRQDWH.

VHFWLRQ 5. JHQHUDO LQIRUPDWLRQ DERXW SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV

SURIHVVRU PLFKDHO V. KDUW ZDV WKH RULJLQDWRU RI WKH SURMHFW
JXWHQEHUJ™ FRQFHSW RI D OLEUDUB RI HOHFWURQLF ZRUNV WKDW FRXOG EH
IUHHOB VKDUHG ZLWK DQBRQH. IRU IRUWB BHDUV, KH SURGXFHG DQG
GLVWULEXWHG SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ HERRNV ZLWK RQOB D ORRVH QHWZRUN RI
YROXQWHHU VXSSRUW.

SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™ HERRNV DUH RIWHQ FUHDWHG IURP VHYHUDO SULQWHG
HGLWLRQV, DOO RI ZKLFK DUH FRQILUPHG DV QRW SURWHFWHG EB FRSBULJKW LQ
WKH X.V. XQOHVV D FRSBULJKW QRWLFH LV LQFOXGHG. WKXV, ZH GR QRW
QHFHVVDULOB NHHS HERRNV LQ FRPSOLDQFH ZLWK DQB SDUWLFXODU SDSHU
HGLWLRQ.

PRVW SHRSOH VWDUW DW RXU ZHEVLWH ZKLFK KDV WKH PDLQ SJ VHDUFK
IDFLOLWB: ZZZ.JXWHQEHUJ.RUJ.

WKLV ZHEVLWH LQFOXGHV LQIRUPDWLRQ DERXW SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ™,
LQFOXGLQJ KRZ WR PDNH GRQDWLRQV WR WKH SURMHFW JXWHQEHUJ OLWHUDUB
DUFKLYH IRXQGDWLRQ, KRZ WR KHOS SURGXFH RXU QHZ HERRNV, DQG KRZ WR
VXEVFULEH WR RXU HPDLO QHZVOHWWHU WR KHDU DERXW QHZ HERRNV.
